# Metadata Rebuild — Foundation Phase — Execution Status — ARCHIVE

**Archived:** 2026-05-05 after Session 17 (PR 1 shipped to PROD).

This file is the full execution journal for **Sessions 1-17** of the foundation-phase metadata rebuild — covering Gates A/B/C, PR 1 implementation (Tasks 1.0/1.1/1.2/1.3/1.3b/1.4a/1.4b/1.5/1.6), and the PR 1 ritual rounds 1-5 (Sessions 13-17). All content from the active status doc as of session-end on 2026-05-05 is preserved here verbatim.

The active status file at `2026-05-03-metadata-rebuild-foundation-execution-status.md` carries forward only the Current State header + recent-decisions roll-up + pre-PR-2 verification list + pointers. Read this archive on demand when historical context is needed (e.g., `grep -n "<term>" 2026-05-03-metadata-rebuild-foundation-execution-status-archive.md`).

After save+reopen, the pill appeared unselected even though `metadata.activityType = 'cooking'` was present and validated. **Real regression introduced BY this PR's previous fix-ups.** **Fix-up commit `c793d54`** (1 file / +17 / -1): module-scope `reAddActivityTypeSuffix` helper at `ReviewDetail.tsx:114-130` mirroring the save-path strip (`'cooking' → 'cooking-only'`, `'both'` and already-suffixed legacy values pass through unchanged); called at the load site (line 416) before `setMetadata`. Round-trip: load adds suffix → reviewer sees pill highlighted → save strips suffix → DB canonical → load adds suffix again. Symmetric. **20 rejects** documented in commit message + summarized below: (a) **5 pre-existing hygiene** (silent gradeLevel discard `useLessonSearch.ts:53`, `as string[]` cast `searchStore.ts:110`, LessonMetadata vs LessonMetadataValidated optionality drift `types/index.ts:33`, IntSidebar three-subscriptions vs useShallow, complete-review console.error vs `_shared/logger.ts` shim) — pre-existing pattern, not PR-1 regressions, fix in Stage 1 / Phase 2 work tracks; active reviewer surface is ReviewDetail.tsx); (c) **3 false alarms** (Claude long-form HIGH on CRF Select options source — `ALL_FIELD_CONFIGS.culturalResponsivenessFeatures` exists in `filterDefinitions.ts:368-392`, consumed at `ReviewDetail.tsx:1071-1073`; Claude long-form S on `ZOD_FIELD_TO_LABEL` completeness — `Record<K,V>` IS already complete in TypeScript by definition; Claude long-form R on `logger.error → logger.debug` at line 3215 — file is only 1413 lines, no line 3215 exists, AND even at the actual line 508 `logger.error` is appropriate per CLAUDE.md for client-side Zod validation failure with Sentry visibility); (d) **1 defense-in-depth** (`academicIntegration.selected` optional chaining at `lessonToReviewMapper.ts:87` — Zod schema requires `selected: z.array(z.string())` on the object branch at `lessonMetadata.zod.ts:77`; function input type `LessonMetadataValidated` guarantees Zod validation passed; the bot's worry is a non-validated `as` cast bypassing the schema, possible but discouraged by the type signature — round-cap reject); Verified by Session 14's own status doc + git diff. Q2-Q5 (per-finding accept/reject dispositions) → user approved 5 accepts: Q1 (P1 activityType placement) + Q2 (medium CRF CreatableSelect→Select) + Q3a (saveError single-sentence) + Q3b (ZOD_FIELD_TO_LABEL exhaustive type) + Q3c (compat-bridge + tags-badge TODO refs); Q4 (seasonTiming trigger inline comment) + Q5 (everything else) reject; user requested noting the rejects "if useful to return to" — three captured below in Out-of-scope follow-ups. **Fix-up commit `73f7eac`** (3 files / +31 / -16): **(1) P1 — `ReviewDetail.tsx` activityType normalization moved `handleMetadataChange` → `handleSaveReview`.** Build `payload` object with stripped suffix; `safeParse(payload)` (not `safeParse(metadata)`); pass `payload` (not raw `metadata`) into `complete-review` invoke body. Form state stays in UI-slug form so display continues to highlight the selected pill; only the transmitted value is canonical. The redundant `value !== 'both'` guard from Session 14 falls out automatically (was inline in `handleMetadataChange`; new save-path strip uses simple `typeof === 'string'` since `'both'.replace(/-only$/, '')` returns `'both'` unchanged). **(2) MEDIUM — CRF field `CreatableSelect` → non-creatable `<Select isMulti>`** at `ReviewDetail.tsx:1060`. New `import Select from 'react-select'` at top. CRF is a closed enum (7 Brown CR master-list features) enforced by Zod + SQL CHECK in PR 1; CreatableSelect would invite reviewer-typed values that the save path silently rejects. Other 5 `CreatableSelect` usages (heritage / mainIngredients / cookingSkills / gardenSkills / observances) stay creatable — those fields are Stage-1-gated, vocabulary not yet locked in foundation phase. **(3) LOW — `saveError` simplified** at `ReviewDetail.tsx:500`. Replaced `\n`-laden multi-line detail string (which collapses to spaces in HTML — React text node behavior) with single-sentence `'Some fields have invalid values — see highlighted fields above.'`. The `validationErrors` banner at the top already enumerates failing fields with per-IntFormField highlighting. **(4) LOW — `ZOD_FIELD_TO_LABEL` typed as `Record<keyof typeof reviewFormPayloadSchema.shape, string>`** at `ReviewDetail.tsx:93` (was `Record<string, string>`). Compile-time exhaustiveness drift guard — adding a new field to the schema without updating this map is now a tsc error rather than silent runtime fallback. Adjusted call-site `Object.keys(fieldErrors).map((key) => ZOD_FIELD_TO_LABEL[key as keyof typeof ZOD_FIELD_TO_LABEL] ?? key)` to cast through the typed key (?? key fallback preserved for unexpected keys). **(5) LOW — TODO refs.** `useLessonSearch.ts:114` adds `TODO(Task 1.3a):` ref pointing to impl plan §1.3a "Task 1.3a (deferred to next release): drop deprecated parameters". `facetCounts.ts:48` adds TODO ref pointing to status doc Out-of-scope follow-ups → "Lesson Type (tags) facet count badge always shows 0". In-repo doc anchors are the project's tracking convention (no GH issues filed). **Verification:** `npm run type-check` clean; `npm run lint` clean; `npm test --run` 540/540 across 38 files (Session 14 baseline preserved); TS-only changes (no SQL) → per `feedback_per_round_test_db_verification.md` no TEST DB re-verification needed for this round (all 11 round-2 MCP checks remain valid; migration apply state of 20260511120000 / 20260512000000 / 20260515000000 unchanged). **Push:** `git push` successful (`fa4e88b..73f7eac`). **Detailed PR comment posted:** [PR #475#issuecomment-4376464812](https://github.com/danfeder/esnyc-lesson-search-react/pull/475#issuecomment-4376464812) — covers four-surface triage table, 5 accept blocks with file:line + fix-shape, 12 reject table with bot source + reason, verification stats, hygiene follow-ups noted, what's next.

- **PR 1 Task 1.6 — Value-validation guardrails shipped (Session 12, 2026-05-05).** New migration `supabase/migrations/20260515000000_metadata_value_validation.sql` (~430 lines including header + comments) + `.sql.rollback` sibling (~30 lines, inert) + 3-line `supabase/seed.sql` edit (Title-Case `Cooking`/`Gardening` → canonical lowercase `cooking`/`garden` to satisfy the new `valid_activity_type` CHECK on the local seed; same Session 7 precedent of folding seed.sql edits into the Task commit). Migration stages: (1) Pre-CHECK CRF cleanup — idempotent `array_replace` UPDATE on column side + jsonb_agg+CASE rebuild on metadata side, replaces the 1-row drift `'Communication of high expectations'` (singular typo) → `'Communicates high expectations'` on TEST + PROD (verified TEST=1 / PROD=1 row at session start via `mcp__supabase-test__execute_sql` + `mcp__supabase-remote__execute_sql`); (2) Three CHECK constraints on `lessons` text[] columns — `valid_activity_type` (`<@ ARRAY['cooking','garden','both','academic','craft']`), `valid_tags` (`<@ ARRAY['orientation','bilingual_handouts']`), `valid_cultural_responsiveness_features` (`<@` 7-feature master list). All idempotent via DO-block `pg_constraint` existence checks. SOURCE comments cite `enums.json["<key>"]` per validator-arch decision 6; (3) New helper `_validate_meta_enum_values(p_meta jsonb, p_key text, p_allowed text[], p_lesson_id text) RETURNS void` — handles both string-scalar and text-array shapes; no-op on null/absent; RAISE EXCEPTION format: `Invalid value "%s" for metadata.%s; expected one of %s` USING HINT = `Lesson lesson_id=%s` (Decision 3 — user-approved Session 12); (4) `lessons_normalize_write` trigger function CREATE OR REPLACE with new (V) section between (A) rescue and (C)..(K) sync sections — invokes `_validate_meta_enum_values` for THREE keys (`activityType`, `tags`, `culturalResponsivenessFeatures`); placed BEFORE sync sections so drift in metadata raises the structured error message before sync attempts derive a column from it; (5) Final `NOTIFY pgrst, 'reload schema'`. **Decision 1 update — `valid_seasons` CHECK was already in place:** TEST DB schema audit at session start showed `valid_seasons` already enforces `season_timing <@ ARRAY['Fall','Winter','Spring','Summer']` (baseline migration). Net: 3 new CHECKs, not 4. **Decision 2 update — `seasonTiming` excluded from trigger validation:** TEST DB drift audit showed ~213 rows with non-canonical `metadata.seasonTiming` values (154× `'All Seasons'`, 25× `'Beginning of year'`, 16× `'End of year'`, 12× `'year-round'`, 2× `'end-of-year'`, 2× `'winter'` case-mixed, 1× `'Black History Month'`, 1× `'fall'` case-mixed). Hard-failing the trigger on those keys would break reviewer saves on legacy rows; values like `'All Seasons'`/`'year-round'`/`'Beginning of year'` are semantically meaningful concepts that don't fit the 4-season enum and need a Stage 1 worksheet design call (drop / promote to tags / add 'all-year' canonical value). Captured as out-of-scope follow-up below. Local verification: `supabase db reset` initial run failed on the seed `Cooking`/`Gardening` Title-Case values (proves CHECK fires correctly); after seed fix re-run cleanly applied all 59 migrations. Schema verifies via local MCP — all 4 CHECK constraints present (3 new + valid_seasons baseline); both `_validate_meta_enum_values` + `lessons_normalize_write` present with correct signatures; trigger body has the (V) section AND calls helper. 8 smoke tests via MCP: T1 column CHECK rejects bad `activity_type` UPDATE (`valid_activity_type` violation); T2/T3/T4 trigger value-validation rejects bad metadata for activityType / tags / culturalResponsivenessFeatures with EXACT spec'd error messages; T5 seasonTiming drift `["All Seasons"]` SUCCEEDS (silently corrected by existing sync section G to match column `['Spring','Summer']` — confirms exclusion design); T6 valid academic + orientation update succeeds; T7 CRF cleanup idempotent on already-clean data (0 rows column drift / 0 rows metadata drift); T8 helper directly callable returns NULL on valid input. TEST DB sanity check confirms pre-migration state (only `valid_seasons` + `lessons_normalize_write` exist; new CHECKs + helper absent; CI will apply on PR open). `npm run type-check` + `npm run lint` clean; `npm test --run` 537/537 across 38 files (Session 11 baseline preserved); `npm run test:rls` 5 passed / 2 failed (same pre-existing `archive_duplicate_lesson` scenario failures as Sessions 6-11 baseline; Task 1.6 touches no RLS or RPC affecting those scenarios). Branch is local (not pushed); PR 1 multi-task opens after this task lands the commit.
- **PR 1 Task 1.5 — Wire Zod schemas to write surfaces shipped (commit `7b27d03`, 4 files / +322).** First real exercise of the Task 1.0 Zod scaffold's edge-runtime side. Three surfaces wired + one new test artifact: (1) `supabase/functions/complete-review/index.ts` — adds `import { reviewFormPayloadSchema } from '../_shared/metadataSchemas.ts'` + a defense-in-depth `safeParse()` step positioned AFTER existing structural checks (submissionId/decision/selectedLessonId) and BEFORE the embedding-regen and RPC paths; on failure returns 400 with `{ error: 'Invalid metadata shape', fieldErrors, formErrors }` (Zod `.flatten()` output — rich field-level errors per user direction). Skips parse when `metadata` is null/undefined/non-object (RPC accepts `{}` for non-approve decisions). (2) `src/pages/ReviewDetail.tsx` — adds `import { reviewFormPayloadSchema } from '@/types/reviewFormPayload.zod'` + a module-level `ZOD_FIELD_TO_LABEL` map (17 keys → human labels mirroring required-fields labels) + a save-time `safeParse(metadata)` step inserted between the existing required-fields-pass clearing and the `setSaving(true)` line. Existing required-fields banner / save-error banner / scroll-to-top behaviour reused — no UX restructure. Header comment notes the duplication rationale (edge functions can't reliably import from `src/` at deploy time; `_shared/` is the established pattern per `cors.ts`/`search-helpers.ts`). (4) New file `src/types/edgeSharedSchemas.equivalence.test.ts` (~120 lines) — 30-test Vitest suite imports BOTH canonical and shared modules, asserts identical closed-enum value lists across the 4 closed enums (activity_type/tags/season_timing/CRF) + identical `safeParse` behaviour on representative valid/invalid fixtures. Wrapping with `lessonMetadataSchema.parse()` would surface false-positive failures on legitimate legacy shapes the scripts are designed to preserve. Additionally `identify-and-restore-missing-lessons.ts:46-49` has a known activity_type bug (writes `'indoor'`/`'outdoor'` from locationRequirements) that wrapping would expose. All candidate scripts have `requireNonProd` guards so they can never write PROD anyway. The forward-living write coverage is achieved at the edge function (every reviewer save) + frontend (defense-in-depth) layers — those ARE the production write paths. Captured as a session decision (see Decisions section below). **Edge-runtime zod resolution proof:** `supabase functions serve complete-review --no-verify-jwt` boots cleanly with the new zod import. Per-round multi-session pacing precedent (Sessions 7 / 8 / 11 / 13-16): Session 17 likely covers round-5 triage + merge; Session 18 PROD-apply verification.

**Decision points to surface at start of Session 17 (round-cap final, carrying forward from Sessions 14-16):**
- **PR-merge approach.** Squash-merge (`gh pr merge --squash`) collapses the now-12-commit history (8 task commits + 4 fix-ups: `e2134ca` / `36332bc` / `73f7eac` / `c793d54`) into one merge commit on main. Rebase-merge preserves per-task history. Squash is cleaner for main; per-task hashes preserved in PR. Lean: squash, but confirm with user.
- **Tag/release.** PR 1 is one of 6+ PRs in the foundation phase; tagging at PR 1 might be premature. Lean: skip, defer to end-of-foundation-phase tag.
- **PROD-apply scheduling.** Standard pattern. Most-data-affecting migration is the lessonFormat strip (~749 PROD rows). seasonTiming drift on PROD already audited (2 rows, identical to TEST). Manual approval gate is normal.

## Blocked

(none — Stage 1 worksheet round runs in parallel and gates PR 5+ but is not blocking PRs 1-4 / Gates A-C)

## Decisions made during execution

- **2026-05-03 (pre-execution, post-reviewer-feedback round 1):** Three pre-execution gates added (A: lessonFormat dependency sweep verification; B: validator architecture decision + Zod canonical scaffold; C: per-prompt readiness audit). PR breakdown updated: PR 2 ships only vocab-locked prompts (CRF + activity_type + tags + Gate-C-classified); Stage-1-gated prompts deploy after worksheets; PR 3 split into 3a (now) / 3b (after Stage 2). Archive academicConcepts recovery added to PR 4. Validator architecture confirmed Option B (TS/Zod canonical, Pydantic mirrors enums via enums.json, SQL CHECK + trigger value-validation hand-synced).
- **2026-05-03 (factual correction):** Design doc's "9 JSON-path indexes referencing lessonFormat" was wrong — there is 1 JSON-path index (`idx_lessons_format`) + 1 column-based index (`idx_lessons_lesson_format`). The "9" came from conflating the foundational report's 10-element list of metadata-path indexes (one per field — themes/cultures/seasons/etc.). Corrected.
- **2026-05-03 (post-reviewer-feedback round 2):** Three additional P1 fixes:
  - **search_lessons compatibility bridge.** PostgREST returns hard `PGRST202` 404 on unknown RPC params + Netlify 1-year asset cache + 5-min TanStack Query staleTime → stale browser tabs can emit old `filter_lesson_format` after column drop. Pattern: keep deprecated params with `DEFAULT NULL` for one release; drop in Task 1.3a follow-up migration ≥24-48h after frontend deploys. Applies to `search_lessons.filter_lesson_format` parameter + `lessons_with_metadata` view's `lesson_format` projection.
  - **Two-schema Zod architecture.** `LessonMetadata` (canonical, array values, `thematicCategories`/`seasonTiming`/`locationRequirements` keys) and `ReviewMetadata` (review-form, single-select strings, `themes`/`season`/`location` keys) genuinely diverge. Translation today happens server-side in `complete_review_atomic`. Foundation phase ships TWO Zod schemas + bidirectional mappers (`reviewToLesson` + `lessonToReview`) mirroring the SQL translation. Edge functions need `supabase/functions/deno.json` with `"imports": { "zod": "npm:zod@3" }` (or fallback URL imports). `zod` not currently in package.json; gets installed in Task 1.0.
  - **LLM draft storage contract.** New columns `lesson_submissions.{ai_draft_metadata jsonb, ai_draft_generated_at timestamptz, ai_draft_model text}` (Option A; Option B rejected because `submission_reviews.reviewer_id` FK NOT NULL to `auth.users` blocks sentinel reviewer). Drafts stored in canonical-keys shape; ReviewDetail.tsx reads at form-init via `lessonToReviewMapper`. `complete_review_atomic` unchanged.
- **2026-05-03 (factual fix):** PR 4 Task 4.5 (FSA retitle) used `WHERE id = '<lesson_id>'` — wrong because `lessons` has both `id uuid` PK and separate `lesson_id text` UNIQUE column; FSA's identifier is the Google Doc ID (text). Frontend keys lessons by `lesson_id` everywhere. Corrected to `WHERE lesson_id = '<FSA lesson_id_text>'`.
- **2026-05-03 (test plan corrections):** Synonym-expansion verification moved from PR 3a manual smoke (where `search_synonyms` is not populated) to PR 3b / PR 6+. Series-aware dedup E2E test removed entirely — design doc §11 explicitly puts dedup-pipeline third-state redesign in a separate work track; series_id columns are scaffolding for that future track, not exercised in foundation phase.
- **2026-05-03 (Session 4 / Task 1.0):** LessonMetadata Zod schema is fully optional (matches runtime usage of partial drafts / legacy rows). Existing `src/types/index.ts` interfaces (some required fields) NOT touched — consumers using the schema get the Zod-inferred type (`LessonMetadataValidated`), consumers using existing interfaces are unaffected. The eventual canonical-source migration (Zod replaces interfaces) is a Phase-2 / out-of-scope decision per validator-architecture doc TBD #2.
- **2026-05-03 (Session 4 / Task 1.0):** Zod resolved at `^3.25.76` from `npm install zod@^3.24.0` (newest 3.x; specifier in deno.json keeps `npm:zod@3.24.0` as the documented baseline since edge runtime resolves loosely). Edge-function smoke verification (`supabase functions serve` boots without zod import errors) deferred to Task 1.5 — no edge function imports zod yet, so deno.json zod resolution isn't exercised until Task 1.5 wires `complete-review` and `process-submission` to the schemas.
- **2026-05-04 (Session 7 / Task 1.3):** `seed.sql` edit folded into Task 1.3 commit even though Gate A bins it under Task 1.3b. Rationale: `supabase db reset` runs seed.sql after migrations; without the edit, db reset fails after the column drop (the seed's INSERT references the dropped lesson_format column). It's a verification dependency for Task 1.3, not a clean separation. Captured as a Session 7 amendment in this doc; no impact on Task 1.3b's remaining work.
- **2026-05-04 (Session 7 / Task 1.3):** Q5 verification query in impl plan §1.3 — `pg_get_functiondef(...) ~ 'lesson_format'` for complete_review_atomic — produces a false positive because `pg_get_functiondef` includes inline `--`-style comments verbatim, and the new function body has comment markers like `-- lesson_format = COALESCE(...) removed — D3` that legitimately match. Replaced for actual verification with a comment-stripped regex (`regexp_replace(body, '--[^\n]*', '', 'g')` then check). Both complete_review_atomic and search_lessons confirmed clean of functional `lesson_format` refs after stripping comments. Future task-level verifications should use the comment-stripped pattern when checking removed refs in plpgsql function bodies.
- **2026-05-04 (Session 8 / Task 1.3b):** Three Task-1.3b implementation refinements landed during the sweep, two of them divergences from Gate A's literal text that the user blessed at session start:
  - **`searchStore.test.ts` "should handle single-select dropdown filters" test deleted whole rather than per-Gate-A's "delete 4 fixture lines."** Reasoning: the entire `it(...)` block was constructed AROUND lessonFormat single-select behavior (test name + payload + assertions). Surgical 4-line removal would have left an empty `setFilters({})` followup with zero assertions. The cookingMethods value tested in the same payload is multi-select (string[]) not single-select; coverage redundant with other `setFilters` tests in the file. Net test count delta: 508 → 507. Captured as a session decision because the impl plan / Gate A both expected mechanical line removal.
  - **`useLessonSearch.ts:115` compat-bridge handling.** Gate A wording was "DELETE projection; KEEP RPC param send for one release (compat bridge: send `undefined` always — RPC param has DEFAULT NULL)." Resolved as: deleted the projection (line 49), kept the RPC param entry but changed value to literal `undefined` (line 114 post-edit) with a one-line `// PR 1 compat bridge: keep until Task 1.3a follow-up drops the RPC param.` comment. The comment is justified per `feedback_bot_review_investigation.md` since the line otherwise looks like dead code that reviewer agents would suggest removing. Note: dropping the line entirely would have been functionally equivalent (PostgREST treats omitted-key the same as `undefined`-value), but Gate A specifically asked to KEEP the send for one release as defensive habit.
  - **`scripts/orphan-recovery/phase-5-b-new-publish.ts` decision point resolved.** Gate A flagged this as "User confirmation requested at PR 1 task time." User direction at session start was to follow Gate A recommendation (leave-with-comment). Implemented: 7-line audit notice appended to the existing docstring (lines 3-8) noting `lessons.lesson_format` + `metadata.lessonFormat` were dropped in foundation-phase PR 1, that the script ran once during Phase 5b orphan recovery, and that references are intentionally preserved so the audit record matches PROD-applied SQL. Body untouched.
  - **lesson-search.infinite.test.tsx replace_all gotcha (process learning).** First `replace_all` Edit caught only 2 of 5 lessonFormat fixture refs because the file has TWO indentation depths — the simpler test (lines 51-56) uses 12-space indent for inner metadata fields, the nested mockResolvedValueOnce.mockResolvedValueOnce calls (lines 103+, 118+, 138+) use 14-space indent. Required a second `replace_all` with the deeper-indent pattern. Lesson: when files have multiply-nested fixtures, verify with grep after each replace_all that all expected refs are gone before moving on.
  - **Two now-unused declarations removed during type-check fix-up:** `setFilters` destructure in IntSidebar (line 31; only the deleted lessonFormat radio used it) + `asString` helper in useLessonSearch's normalizeMetadata (line 41; only the deleted lessonFormat field used it). Both flagged by tsc; removed without ceremony since they were genuine dead references.
- **2026-05-04 (Session 9 / Task 1.4 investigation + split):** Code-explorer agent (Opus) traced the Activity Type filter pipeline and the `search_lessons` RPC signature in current code. Three findings, all of which expanded Task 1.4's scope beyond the impl plan's "frontend-only" framing:
  - **Activity Type filter is NOT broken in production.** The slug-vs-corpus mismatch flagged at Session 8 handoff is bridged by the server-side translator `_alias_activity_type` (`20260505000000_filter_drift_pr1_column_based_search_lessons.sql:72-91`), which expands `'cooking-only'` to match either `'cooking-only'` or `'cooking'`. Adding `craft` requires both a new filter slug AND a new translator branch — they ship together as Task 1.4a (split decision below). Implication: 1.4a is a SQL+frontend change, not just frontend.
  - **`search_lessons` does NOT accept any tags-related parameter today.** Full param list at `20260512000000_drop_lesson_format.sql:148-163` has 14 entries, none touching `lessons.tags`. The new "Lesson Type" sidebar section can't filter without a SQL migration adding `filter_tags text[] DEFAULT NULL`. Because adding a parameter changes the function signature, this requires DROP+CREATE (same pattern as the cooking_methods text→text[] change at `20260505000000:193-208`). Implication: 1.4b is a substantial SQL+frontend change.
  - **`academic-cooking` slug doesn't exist.** Verified absent from current code. The impl plan's "rename `academic-cooking` slug to align with `both` storage" sub-task is moot — nothing to rename. Dropped from scope.
  - **Decision: split Task 1.4 into 1.4a (Activity Type 5-value expand) + 1.4b (Lesson Type tag filter).** Each gets its own SQL migration + own commit + own verification cycle. 1.4a first (smaller blast radius, helps re-warm-up to the migration pattern); 1.4b after. User confirmed split + slug naming `'craft-only'` (Option A — symmetric with `cooking-only` / `garden-only` / `academic-only`, requires new translator entry) over `'craft'` (Option B — would have matched corpus directly, no translator needed). User direction: keep the facet-counts-badge + card-label findings as tracked follow-ups (see "Out-of-scope follow-ups captured here").
  - **Process note: code-explorer agent investigation pattern works well for these "trace through 3-5 surfaces" questions.** Took ~3 minutes, returned file:line evidence for all three questions, surfaced two related quirks that hadn't been on the question list. Pattern reusable when impl-plan task scope feels under-specified before starting.

## Out-of-scope follow-ups captured here

- **`metadata.seasonTiming` JSON-blob drift — ~213 rows on TEST as of 2026-05-05 (Session 12).** Distribution at audit time: 154× `'All Seasons'`, 25× `'Beginning of year'`, 16× `'End of year'`, 12× `'year-round'`, 2× `'end-of-year'`, 2× `'winter'` (case-mixed lowercase), 1× `'Black History Month'`, 1× `'fall'` (case-mixed lowercase). Surfaced during Task 1.6 trigger-scope decision audit. **Rejected from Task 1.6 scope** because hard-failing trigger validation on those keys would break reviewer saves on ~213 legacy rows (the trigger fires on every UPDATE regardless of whether seasonTiming is being changed). Existing baseline `valid_seasons` CHECK still protects the column-side; this drift lives only in metadata. Three substantive value classes: (a) **structural-mismatch values** (`'All Seasons'`, `'year-round'`) — semantically valid but don't fit the 4-season canonical enum; need a Stage 1 worksheet decision (drop / promote to `tags` / add `'all-year'` canonical / split-into-multiple); (b) **time-of-year values** (`'Beginning of year'`, `'End of year'`, `'Black History Month'`) — possibly belong in a different field entirely (observances/holidays/calendar-event); (c) **case-mixing typos** (`'fall'` / `'winter'` lowercase, `'end-of-year'` kebab) — mechanical canonicalization. **Path to fix:** Stage 1 seasonTiming worksheet round (curriculum-team-driven) decides canonical handling per-class; D4 vocab canonicalization migration cleans rows accordingly; trigger value-validation extended to seasonTiming once corpus is clean. **Earliest:** PR 5+. Until then, `metadata.seasonTiming` drift is preserved as-is on PROD (existing trigger sync silently corrects when the column has canonical data; rows where column is NULL are write-broken today regardless of Task 1.6 — pre-existing).
- **Lesson Type (tags) facet count badge always shows 0 (Session 10).** Different shape from the Activity Type bug: not a slug-vs-corpus mismatch, but a "no per-row data source" issue. Cause: `search_lessons` RPC's `RETURNS TABLE` does not expose `lessons.tags` as a top-level field (and `tags` is not a metadata key, so it's not picked up by the per-field COALESCE metadata reconstruction either). `facetCounts.ts` therefore has no signal for tags; `valuesForKey('tags')` returns `[]` intentionally with a code comment explaining why. **Filter itself works correctly end-to-end** via the new WHERE clause — only the badge count is wrong (and only the badge — sidebar checkboxes still toggle and still filter results). **Fix shape (future, post-PR-2 once tags are populated):** add `tags text[]` to the `RETURNS TABLE` shape of `search_lessons` (requires another DROP+CREATE), update `useLessonSearch.normalizeMetadata` or add a top-level `tags` to the Lesson type, then read `lesson.tags` in `valuesForKey('tags')`. Alternatively (cheaper but conceptually mixed) inject `tags` into the per-field metadata reconstruction COALESCE block so it arrives under `metadata.tags`. Captured 2026-05-04 by Session 10 as a deliberate scope-discipline decision — same caliber follow-up as the Activity Type badge bug.
- **Activity Type facet count badge bug (pre-existing).** The "(43)" number rendered next to each Activity Type filter checkbox always shows zero. Cause: `facetCounts.ts` groups corpus values (`cooking` / `garden` / `academic` / `both`) into buckets keyed by raw column value, but the lookup at `IntSidebar.tsx:91` keys by filter slug (`cooking-only` / `garden-only` / `academic-only` / `both`). The slug-vs-corpus axis mismatch means buckets and lookups never match for three of the four values; only `both` happens to align. Filter behavior itself is correct (the `_alias_activity_type` helper bridges it server-side); only the badge count is wrong. **Fix shape:** key the count lookup by raw column value (or apply the same alias translation on the count side). Small frontend-only change once we touch facetCounts again. Surfaced 2026-05-04 by Session 9 code-explorer investigation. Do not lose track — visible UX bug.
- **Card-side Activity Type label uses different signal than the filter.** `intActivityLabel` in `IntListRow.tsx:13-20` (consumed by `IntCard.tsx:13`) computes the card badge ("Cook" / "Grow" / "Cook + Grow" / "Academic") from `meta.cookingSkills.length` and `meta.gardenSkills.length` — the `activity_type` column is never consulted. Adding `craft-only` to the filter in 1.4a does NOT produce a "Craft" badge on cards. Out-of-scope per impl plan §1.4 framing, but worth a follow-up sweep if/when craft lessons are imported, so the badge axis matches the filter axis.
- **Equivalence test could assert key-presence symmetrically (Session 15 round-2 reject from claude long-form #1 #6).** `src/types/edgeSharedSchemas.equivalence.test.ts` currently compares `.data` objects from canonical and Deno-mirror parsers. If a field were accidentally deleted from BOTH schemas, the test passes (both `.data` match). A `Object.keys(canonicalResult.data).forEach(k => expect(sharedResult.data).toHaveProperty(k))` assertion would catch the symmetric-deletion drift mode. Rejected for round-3 fix-up (existing test catches behavioral drift via `safeParse` + value comparison; symmetric-deletion is narrow). **Worth returning to** when Stage 2 re-tag scaffolding adds new fields — per-PR-2 batch additions could trip this mode. ~3-line test addition; cheap to do then.
- **Hand-patched `database.types.ts` — heads-up for next full regen sweep (Session 15 round-2 reject from claude long-form #1 #9).** Three columns (`series_id`, `part_number`, `crf_confirmed`) + one RPC arg (`filter_tags`) were added manually to `src/types/database.types.ts` in `e2134ca` (Session 13 fix-up) per repo precedent (commits `249e7df` / `b39eb92` are the same pattern — the supabase CLI's full regen produces 3000+ line cosmetic diffs from version drift). When the next full regen sweep happens, the regen will silently drop these patches if the operator doesn't preserve them. Mitigation at regen time: diff against `database.types.ts` pre-regen for `series_id` / `part_number` / `crf_confirmed` / `filter_tags` and re-apply if missing. Could ship a top-of-file comment listing the manual additions; not done in round 3 because no regen is scheduled and the bot's reasoning ("future regen sweep" speculation) doesn't have a date.
- **GIN index on `lessons.tags` — future scale follow-up (Session 15 round-2 reject from claude long-form #2 #3).** PR 1 introduced `filter_tags text[]` overlap query (`l.tags && filter_tags`) at `search_lessons`. For 831 corpus rows + ~20 currently populated tag rows, sequential scan is fine. Rejected for foundation phase. **Worth returning to** when PR 2's submission-time auto-tag starts populating tags at scale (post-PR 2 corpus could grow to several hundred populated rows quickly if `orientation` + `bilingual_handouts` apply broadly). Form: `CREATE INDEX CONCURRENTLY lessons_tags_gin ON lessons USING GIN (tags) WHERE tags IS NOT NULL;` — partial GIN to keep the index small while corpus is sparsely populated. Schedule after PR 2 ships and we have row-count signal.

### Decision points raised by sweep

1. **`lesson_archive.lesson_format` column** — KEEP per Gate A default. The archive table preserves historical metadata; only the source side (`lessons.lesson_format` SELECT in `archive_duplicate_lesson` + `resolve_duplicate_group`) needs rewriting. Document in PR 1 commit. **Session 5 confirmation:** TEST DB columns query confirmed both `lessons.lesson_format` and `lesson_archive.lesson_format` exist as separate text-nullable columns.
2. **`resolve_duplicate_group` is a 5th RPC** — fold into PR 1 Task 1.3 step 2. Same INSERT-into-lesson_archive pattern as archive_duplicate_lesson; same fix (rewrite source side).
3. **`scripts/orphan-recovery/phase-5-b-new-publish.ts`** — historical recovery script that ran during Phase 5b. Recommend leaving with a header comment rather than removing references (script won't re-run; audit value preserved). User confirmation requested at PR 1 task time.
4. **`supabase/dump-data.sql`** — pg_dump output sitting in source control; not referenced by `seed.sql` or supabase config. The 993 lessonFormat hits are data values, not code. NO ACTION.
5. **`scripts/migrate-metadata-to-columns.mjs`** — appears to be a historical column-migration helper script (writes lesson_format alongside other columns). DELETE entries since the script may need reuse for future column migrations; cleaner to keep it consistent with current schema.

### Session 5 amendments — additional findings (2026-05-04)

6. **Snapshot JSON data files (5 files / 41 line refs) — NO ACTION** (per `dump-data.sql` precedent). Files: `scripts/orphan-recovery/snapshots/multi-review-pre-20260427.json` (33 refs) + `category-b-update-*-pre.json` × 4 (2 refs each = 8 refs). These are pre-recovery JSON snapshots taken 2026-04-27 archiving live row state for forensics; the `lessonFormat` keys/values are data, not code. Same disposition as `supabase/dump-data.sql`'s 993 hits.

7. **Session-4 Zod scaffold added 13 new lessonFormat refs across 5 files — fold into Task 1.3b removal list:**

   | File | Lines | Action |
   |---|---|---|
   | `src/types/lessonMetadata.zod.ts` | 110-112 (comment block "Single-string fields. lessonFormat drops in PR 1 Task 1.3 (D3); included…"), 113 (`lessonFormat: z.string().optional()`) | DELETE comment + field declaration |
   | `src/types/reviewFormPayload.zod.ts` | 37 (`lessonFormat: z.string().optional()`) | DELETE |
   | `src/utils/reviewToLessonMapper.ts` | 81-82 (translation block: `if (input.lessonFormat) { out.lessonFormat = input.lessonFormat; }`) | DELETE |
   | `src/utils/lessonToReviewMapper.ts` | 93-94 (translation block: `if (input.lessonFormat) { out.lessonFormat = input.lessonFormat; }`) | DELETE |
   | `src/utils/reviewToLessonMapper.test.ts` | 72, 77, 98, 119, 215, 239 (6 fixture lines, mostly `'Standalone'` + 1 `'Single period'`) | DELETE field from each fixture (not the test cases themselves; the round-trip tests still cover other fields after lessonFormat removal) |

   These were intentionally included in the Task 1.0 scaffold per Session 4 decision ("Scaffold matches CURRENT TS interfaces; field disappears with the column drop"); Task 1.3b is where the disappearance happens.

8. **Legacy `handle_lessons_metadata_write_trg` confirmed NOT attached on TEST DB.** Triggers query showed only `lessons_normalize_write_trg` (the M4 trigger Task 1.3 step 3 rewrites) and `update_lesson_search_vector_trigger` (search vector — not lessonFormat-related). **Task 1.3 step 7 ("Drop legacy `handle_lessons_metadata_write` trigger if still attached") downgraded to verification-only no-op** — re-run the same query during Task 1.3 implementation to reconfirm before omitting the DROP TRIGGER statement.

9. **`cultural_responsiveness_features` 1-row drift requires Task 1.6 attention.** TEST DB distribution shows 7 master-list values (cnt 68→417) + 1 drift row "Communication of high expectations" (cnt=1 — singular typo of "Communicates"). The Task 1.6 CHECK constraint as currently spec'd (`<@ ARRAY[...7 master-list features...]`) would FAIL on this row. **Recommendation:** fold a 1-row UPDATE into the Task 1.6 migration BEFORE the CHECK installs (within the same transaction): `UPDATE lessons SET cultural_responsiveness_features = array_replace(cultural_responsiveness_features, 'Communication of high expectations', 'Communicates high expectations') WHERE 'Communication of high expectations' = ANY(cultural_responsiveness_features);` — idempotent; running twice is a no-op once cleaned. Alternative: lenient CHECK that accepts the drift value (worse — it preserves Stage-2 cleanup cost). Verify on PROD via `mcp__supabase-remote__execute_sql` at PR 1 PROD-apply time; cleanup count will likely be ≤1 row in PROD too.

### Session 5 — TEST DB verification results (queries from "TEST DB verification needed at PR 1 task time" above, all run 2026-05-04)

| # | Query intent | Result |
|---|---|---|
| 1 | Triggers attached to `lessons` | `lessons_normalize_write_trg` (active) + `update_lesson_search_vector_trigger` (active, unrelated). **`handle_lessons_metadata_write_trg` NOT attached** — Task 1.3 step 7 downgraded to no-op (per amendment 8 above). |
| 2 | lessonFormat indexes | 2 indexes: `idx_lessons_format` (JSON-path on `metadata->>'lessonFormat'`) + `idx_lessons_lesson_format` (column-based on `lesson_format`). **Matches Gate A inventory exactly.** |
| 3 | lessonFormat data populations | Total 772 rows; 749 have `metadata.lessonFormat` key; 748 have `lessons.lesson_format` column populated; 748 have BOTH. ~97% population both sides; 1-row mismatch (metadata key but null column) negligible since Task 1.3 strips both. |
| 4 | activity_type distribution | 5 distinct values: `{cooking}` 298 / `{garden}` 278 / `{both}` 135 / `{academic}` 58 / `{}` 3 (empty). Total 772 ✓. **All populated rows are single-element text[]; ZERO rows currently use `craft`** — D2 fifth value safe to add to CHECK constraint. |
| 5 | tags column usage | 752 NULL + 20 empty array + 0 populated = 772 ✓. Column unused in production data. **CHECK `tags <@ ARRAY['orientation','bilingual_handouts']` passes universally** (empty subset is always true). |
| 6 | CRF distribution + drift | 7 master-list values present (cnt 68→417) + **1 drift row "Communication of high expectations" cnt=1** — singular typo of "Communicates". See amendment 9 above for Task 1.6 cleanup recommendation. |

### Session 7 amendments — TEST DB + migration-history reality check (2026-05-04)

10. **`archive_duplicate_lesson` is NO-OP for Task 1.3.** Gate A predicted this RPC needs source-side rewriting (because 20251205/06/07/08 versions had `lesson_format` in INSERT INTO lesson_archive). Session 7 verified on TEST DB via `pg_get_functiondef('public.archive_duplicate_lesson'::regproc) ~ 'lesson_format'` → returns `false`. The active definition is `20260209140001_cleanup_archive_function.sql` lines 13-114 — the cleanup migration removed both `duplicate_pairs` (its stated purpose) and `lesson_format` (incidentally, by writing a leaner INSERT that omits both). Net: no redefinition needed in Task 1.3. The function continues to populate `lesson_archive.metadata` (jsonb) but does NOT populate `lesson_archive.lesson_format` text column — consistent with the Gate A keep-historical decision (existing archive rows keep their values; new archives get NULL).

11. **`resolve_duplicate_group` is NO-OP for Task 1.3 — function was DROPped pre-foundation-phase.** Gate A predicted this RPC needs the same source-side rewrite as `archive_duplicate_lesson`. Session 7 verified absent from `pg_proc` on both TEST DB AND PROD DB (queried 2026-05-04). The drop happened in `20251205_add_archive_duplicate_lesson_function.sql` line 190: `DROP FUNCTION IF EXISTS resolve_duplicate_group(...)`. The 20251205 migration replaced the complex group-resolution flow with the simpler per-lesson `archive_duplicate_lesson`. Gate A's prediction was based on the existence of the 20251203 + 20251204 migration files (which CREATE OR REPLACE the function), not on the active DB state — the deletion in the immediately-following 20251205 migration was missed during the file-based sweep. Net: no redefinition needed; function does not exist to redefine.

**Net effect on Task 1.3 RPC scope:** 3 active redefinitions instead of Gate A's predicted 5. Task 1.3 file is correspondingly leaner. Future surface sweeps that enumerate RPCs from migration files should also probe `pg_proc` to catch dropped definitions.

## Gate C output — Per-prompt readiness audit (Session 3, 2026-05-03)

### Verdict

10 candidate fields evaluated. **5 vocab-locked / 5 Stage-1-gated / 0 dropped.** Combined with design-doc-locked classifications (CRF / activity_type / tags vocab-locked + academicConcepts / cultural_heritage Stage-1-gated), the **PR 2 vocab-locked prompt scope is 8 prompts**; **Stage-1-gated prompt scope is 6 distinct prompts** (post-bundling of academicConcepts+academic_integration into one consolidated subject+concepts prompt per user decision Q2).

Two obvious-gap candidates surfaced during audit and added to the list per user direction:
- **`core_competencies`** — same structural shape as `social_emotional_learning` / `thematic_categories` (closed Title-Case enum + kebab dupes); was missed from impl plan §Gate C list. User confirmed addition (vocab-locked).
- **`academic_integration` (top-level subjects)** — clean 6-value v3 enum + kebab dupes. Mechanically vocab-locked, BUT operationally tied to `academicConcepts` (D5 locked Stage-1-gated). User confirmed bundling: one consolidated submission-time prompt does a single body-read and outputs both top-level subjects AND nested concepts; the bundled prompt waits for the concepts worksheet.

### Method

- TEST DB queried via `mcp__supabase-test__execute_sql` (corpus = 772 lessons; matches PROD shape per `project_metadata_three_regimes.md`).
- Each field's distinct-value count, total appearances, top-N values, and case-mix indicators read out.
- Compared against v3 baseline at `/Users/danfeder/cCode/taggingv3/esynyc-taxonomy-schema-v2.md` and drift signals at `project_vocabulary_drift_scope.md`.
- Classification framework: **vocab-locked** = vocabulary is unambiguous today (matches v3, no novel concepts the corpus surfaces beyond minor case-drift dupes); **Stage-1-gated** = vocabulary needs ontology decisions (novel concepts beyond v3 / category-headers tagged as values / group-vs-specific granularity ambiguity) requiring curriculum-team validation in a worksheet round; **dropped** = out of foundation-phase scope.

| 9 | `observances_holidays` | 17 | 129 (sparse — 17% of corpus) | **Stage-1-gated** | smaller-fields (small) | 10 v3 + 5 sensible corpus additions (Juneteenth 4 / Eid 3 / Earth month 2 / Pride 1 / New Year 1); **chose Stage-1-gated for discipline per Q3** (downgrade to vocab-locked acceptable if curriculum team waves it through quickly) |
| 10 | `academic_integration` (top-level subjects) | 12 | 1369 | **Stage-1-gated** (BUNDLED) | concepts | 6 v3 subjects + 6 kebab dupes; **bundled with `academicConcepts` per Q2** — single consolidated submission-time prompt, one body-read, two outputs (subjects array + concepts object). Top-level technically vocab-locked today, but operational efficiency wins. |

### Net PR 2 prompt scope (post-Gate-C)

**Vocab-locked (8 prompts, ship in PR 2 once eval gate passes for each):**
1. `cultural_responsiveness_features` (D9; 7 master-list features)
2. `activity_type` (D2; 5 values)
3. `tags` (D2+D7; 2 values)
4. `thematic_categories` (Gate C; 7 values)
5. `social_emotional_learning` (Gate C; 5 CASEL values)
6. `cooking_methods` (Gate C; 4 values)
7. `season_timing` (Gate C; 4 values)
8. `core_competencies` (Gate C; 6 ESYNYC values)

**Stage-1-gated (6 distinct prompts, deploy after corresponding worksheet lands):**

| Worksheet round | Prompts gated by it |
|---|---|
| **heritage** | `cultural_heritage` (1 prompt) |
| **concepts** | `academicConcepts` + `academic_integration` BUNDLED (1 consolidated prompt) |
| **smaller-fields** | `garden_skills`, `cooking_skills`, `main_ingredients`, `observances_holidays` (4 prompts) |

Total post-bundling: **6 distinct Stage-1-gated prompts** rather than the 7 a fully-split design would have implied.

### Decisions captured (Gate C)

- **Q1 — `core_competencies` added.** Pattern matches `social_emotional_learning` exactly: 6 ESYNYC official Title-Case values + 6 kebab dupes + 1 rogue value; mechanical canonicalization. Was missed from impl plan §Gate C list.
- **Q2 — academic_integration top-level + academicConcepts bundled.** Single consolidated submission-time prompt: one LLM body-read, two outputs (subjects array + nested concepts object). Avoids the 2× LLM call cost of splitting them. Bundle waits for the concepts worksheet (Stage-1-gated category dominates).
- **Q3 — `observances_holidays` Stage-1-gated, not vocab-locked.** Mostly canonical today + 5 sensible corpus additions; could have shipped vocab-locked with the corpus list. Chose Stage-1-gated for "every vocab gets curriculum-validated" discipline. Downgrade to vocab-locked is acceptable if curriculum team rubber-stamps the additions quickly.

### TEST DB verification at PR 2 task time (forward-looking)

Before each Stage-1-gated prompt deploys post-worksheet, re-query the corpus to confirm:
1. Worksheet output (canonical vocab + alias list) covers every distinct value currently in the field.
2. Any drift introduced between PR 2 ship and worksheet land is captured in alias map for Stage 2 re-tag mapping.
3. For `academic_integration` BUNDLED prompt: subjects + concepts arrive consistently in canonical-keys shape; mapper tests cover the bundle.

### Notes for PR 2 implementation planner

- Per the operational gating choice (kickoff §LOCKED): vocab-locked prompts ship in PR 2 only after their per-prompt eval gate passes. Plan 8 eval-gate runs in PR 2 task list, not 3.
- Per `academicConcepts` bundling: PR 2's prompt-design doc should include one consolidated `academic_integration` prompt spec (subjects + concepts), not two; the bundled prompt's vocabulary scope is gated by the concepts worksheet outputs.
- The 6 `cooking_skills` v3 category headers ("Cutting Skills", "Basic Skills", "Cooking Techniques", "Presentation", "Cutting Skills" sub-categories) being tagged as if they're skill values is itself a worksheet input — surfaces the question "do we expose v3 categories as skills, collapse them, or split into a 2-level taxonomy?"
- The 5 corpus observances additions (Juneteenth / Eid / Earth month / Pride / New Year) are pre-staged inputs for the smaller-fields worksheet — they're already in PROD-ish data, the worksheet just blesses-or-trims.

### Session 6 — 2026-05-04 — PR 1 Task 1.2 (additive schema migration shipped)

Major events:
- **Migration committed as `eaaf702` on `feat/metadata-foundation-schema`** (1 file, +55 lines). File: `supabase/migrations/20260511000000_metadata_foundation_schema_additive.sql`.
- **Filename selection.** Latest existing migration was `20260510000000_approve_update_concepts_carry_forward.sql`; chose `20260511000000_*` to sort cleanly after it (per MEMORY.md ASCII-sort gotcha — `YYYYMMDD_*` sorts AFTER `YYYYMMDDHHMMSS_*` in ASCII because `_` > digits, so any same-day timestamped variant alongside an existing `YYYYMMDD_` file requires next-day to ensure correct sort order; not directly applicable here since all baseline-era migrations use `YYYYMMDDHHMMSS` already, but the next-day choice keeps things unambiguous).
- **Migration shape (per impl plan §1.2):**
  - `ALTER TABLE lessons ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS series_id text` (nullable, default NULL — D6).
  - `ALTER TABLE lessons ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS part_number int` (nullable, default NULL — D6).
  - `ALTER TABLE lessons ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS crf_confirmed boolean NOT NULL DEFAULT false` (D9; PG ≥11 handles default-backfill via constant-default optimization without full-table rewrite).
  - Two partial indexes: `lessons_series_id_idx WHERE series_id IS NOT NULL` + `lessons_part_number_idx WHERE part_number IS NOT NULL` (sparse columns; only index populated rows).
  - Rollback block included as comments (drop indexes → drop columns, reverse-order).
  - Every statement `IF NOT EXISTS` — safe to re-run.
- **Local verification (per `supabase db reset` + MCP):**
  - `supabase db reset` succeeded; all migrations including the new one applied cleanly. Final NOTICE messages were the expected `lessons_normalize_write` coercions on the 5 seed lessons (unrelated to Task 1.2).
  - `mcp__supabase__execute_sql` schema inspection — `information_schema.columns` confirmed: `crf_confirmed boolean NOT NULL DEFAULT false`, `part_number integer NULLABLE`, `series_id text NULLABLE`. Exactly as spec'd.
  - `pg_indexes` confirmed: both partial indexes present with correct WHERE clauses.
  - Data check — 5 seed rows; 0 populated for series_id and part_number (expected); all 5 rows have `crf_confirmed=false` (DEFAULT applied correctly; 0 NULLs, 0 TRUE).
  - Idempotency verified — re-ran the entire migration body (3 ALTER + 2 CREATE INDEX) directly via MCP; all `IF NOT EXISTS` clauses no-op'd cleanly. Confirms PR 1 PROD-apply rerun safety (per the SASL-flake mitigation pattern in MEMORY.md — apply-step variant).
- **`supabase db diff` could not run** — shadow-DB port-conflict (port 54320 already bound by another local Supabase project on the user's machine). Unrelated to Task 1.2; the `db reset` + MCP schema-inspection path already covers the same verification surface (compares actual DB state against the migration set). No remediation needed for this migration.
- **RLS verification.** `npm run test:rls` final verdict "✅ RLS implementation is working correctly!" — 16/16 tables RLS-enabled, 16/16 with policies. Two pre-existing scenario failures in `archive_duplicate_lesson` validation (`validates lesson existence`, `prevents self-archiving`) — unrelated to Task 1.2 (additive columns only, no RLS / RPC changes). Captured here for visibility but not regression-introduced; verify against baseline if they resurface in a later RPC-touching task (Task 1.3 redefines `archive_duplicate_lesson` as part of the lessonFormat sweep, so these failures may resolve incidentally).
- **Baseline checks clean throughout:** `npm run type-check && npm run lint` both green pre-commit and post-commit.

Multi-stage transactional migration covering (1) `CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW lessons_with_metadata` with `NULL::text AS lesson_format` projection (compat bridge for one release per the post-reviewer-feedback round-2 P1 fix); (2) redefine 5 RPCs — `search_lessons` (KEEP `filter_lesson_format text DEFAULT NULL` parameter for compat bridge, REMOVE the WHERE clause that uses `_alias_lesson_format(...)`), `complete_review_atomic` (drop `lesson_format` column refs + `v_meta->>'lessonFormat'`), `get_lesson_details_for_review` (drop column from RETURNS TABLE + SELECT), `archive_duplicate_lesson` + `resolve_duplicate_group` (rewrite source side — Gate A keep-historical default for `lesson_archive.lesson_format`); (3) rewrite `lessons_normalize_write_trg` to drop column⇄metadata sync logic for lessonFormat; (4) drop 2 indexes (`idx_lessons_format` JSON-path + `idx_lessons_lesson_format` column-based); (5) `UPDATE lessons SET metadata = metadata - 'lessonFormat'`; (6) drop column; (7) verify-only no-op for legacy `handle_lessons_metadata_write` trigger (Session 5 confirmed not attached on TEST DB). **Decision points to surface at start of Session 9:**
- **Filter slug-vs-storage alignment.** TEST DB Session 5 audit showed activity_type column stores values matching D2 enum directly (`cooking / garden / both / academic`, no `craft` rows yet). But filterDefinitions.ts uses different slugs (`cooking-only / garden-only / both / academic-only`). The `useLessonSearch` filter passes `activityType` strings directly to `filter_activity_type` RPC param — which then matches against `activity_type` column values. So today's filter slugs don't match storage; either there's a translation layer somewhere (need to find and adjust), or the filter is silently broken. Verify before Task 1.4 ships.
- **`tags` filter UI shape.** `tags` column is text[] (multi-select per Gate C audit row). Sidebar's CHECKBOX_KEYS pattern handles multi-select naturally; just add `tags` to the array + add FILTER_CONFIGS.tags entry. But what's the user-facing label? "Lesson Type" per impl plan §1.4. What's the wiring on `useLessonSearch` for the new param (does `search_lessons` RPC accept a `filter_tags text[]` param yet, or does this need a follow-up RPC change)? Investigation needed at Task 1.4 start; may need to defer the search-end of the tags filter to a separate task if the RPC doesn't support it yet.
- **Whether to fold this into Task 1.4 or split.** Task 1.4 is mostly UI + filter-config changes per impl plan; if RPC support for tags filter is needed, that's a separate SQL migration. Suggest opening Task 1.4 with the UI scope first, then tagging on a Task 1.4a if the RPC needs changes.

Single commit per impl plan §1.4b ("single commit covering the migration + ~7 frontend file edits").
- **Filename selection.** Latest existing migration was `20260513000000_alias_activity_type_add_craft.sql`; chose `20260514000000_*` to sort cleanly after it (one-day-forward convention used in this initiative since Session 6).
- **Two decision points from Session 8 handoff resolved at session start:**
  - **Sidebar slot.** User chose "at the top, or near the top" framing, calling Lesson Type "a pretty big choice." Implemented as: `'tags'` prepended as the FIRST entry of `CHECKBOX_KEYS` in `IntSidebar.tsx:13-23` — i.e., slot 1 in the iterated checkbox-filter array. Visually that lands directly under the bespoke Grade Level pills (which are special-cased and rendered above CHECKBOX_KEYS), above Activity Type. ALSO extended `defaultOpen` condition (line 81 post-edit) to include `'tags'` so the section starts expanded — otherwise the prominence framing would be undermined by the user having to click to expand. Slot-1-and-defaultOpen captures "near the top, prominent" without restructuring the existing Grade Level chrome.
  - **Edge-shared helper symmetry.** Recommended + accepted: plumb `filter_tags` through `_shared/search-helpers.ts` too. Reasoning: two query paths exist (main lesson search via `search_lessons` RPC + edge functions `search-lessons`/`smart-search` via `_shared/search-helpers.ts` querying `lessons_with_metadata` view directly); both consume the same searchStore filter state. Without symmetry, post-PR-2 land would surface a silent asymmetry (main search respects tag filter; smart-search ignores it) once the tags column starts being populated by the LLM auto-tag pipeline. Cost is small (~3 lines: SearchFilters interface entry + `q.overlaps('tags', filters.tags)` clause). Matches the 1.3b precedent which removed lessonFormat from BOTH paths in parallel for the same reason. **Done now is cheaper than chasing the bug later.**
- **Three implementation decisions captured during execution:**
  - **Tags facet count badge: accept always-0, do not expand RPC scope.** The `lessons.tags` column is a top-level field but is NOT exposed in the `search_lessons` RPC's `RETURNS TABLE` shape (and is not a metadata key, so it's also not picked up by the per-field COALESCE metadata reconstruction). `facetCounts.ts` therefore has no per-row signal for tags — `valuesForKey('tags')` returns `[]` intentionally with an in-code comment explaining why. The filter itself still works end-to-end (the WHERE clause filters rows correctly); only the sidebar badge count is wrong. Three options were weighed: (A) accept always-0 (chosen); (B) inject `tags` into the per-field COALESCE metadata reconstruction (badge works but mixes top-level and metadata-key concerns conceptually); (C) add `tags text[]` to the `RETURNS TABLE` shape (clean but requires another DROP+CREATE migration in this same task — scope creep). Picked (A) for scope discipline — same caliber follow-up as the existing Activity Type facet badge bug. Captured as a tracked follow-up in "Out-of-scope follow-ups captured here" above.
  - **`tags: string[]` on SearchFilters as required (not optional).** Mirrors the existing pattern (every multi-select filter is `string[]` not `string[] | undefined`); initialFilters provides the default `[]`. Keeps `filters.tags?.length ? filters.tags : undefined` style consistent with neighbors at the read sites (useLessonSearch / useLessonSuggestions).
  - **Sidebar `defaultOpen` extended for `tags`.** Per the prominence rationale above. Now three sections start open: tags, activityType, seasonTiming.
- **Local verification (per `superpowers:verification-before-completion` + impl plan §1.4b "Verify locally"):**
  - `supabase db reset` → clean apply across all 58 migrations. NOTICE messages were the expected `lessons_normalize_write` coercions on the 5 seed rows (unrelated).

(2) `routine_privileges` confirms GRANT EXECUTE present for `anon` + `authenticated` + `service_role`. (3) `search_lessons(filter_tags := ARRAY['orientation']::text[])` returns 0 rows (empty column today). (4) `search_lessons()` (no filter) returns full 5 seed rows. **Plus transactional smoke** (BEGIN; INSERT temp row `LESSON-TAG-SMOKE` with `tags=['orientation']`; call `search_lessons(filter_tags := ARRAY['orientation','bilingual_handouts'])` → returned 1 matching row via `&&` overlap; ROLLBACK cleaned up). Confirms the WHERE clause is wired up correctly inside the SELECT body, not just the parameter list.

### Session 11 — 2026-05-04 / 2026-05-05 — PR 1 Task 1.5 (Zod write-surface wiring + edge-runtime resolution proof)

Major events:
- **All four Session 10 handoff decision points resolved at session start:**
  - **(1) Zod resolution proof.** `supabase functions serve complete-review --no-verify-jwt` boots cleanly with the new zod import. Edge runtime v1.73.13 (Deno 2.1.4) loaded the function and reached the auth-check handler. `npm:zod@3.24.0` resolves via `supabase/functions/deno.json` — no esm.sh fallback needed. Task 1.0 deferred verification cleared.
  - **(2) 400 error response shape — RICH (user direction).** Edge function returns `{ error: 'Invalid metadata shape', fieldErrors, formErrors }` from `result.error.flatten()`. fieldErrors is `{ [fieldName]: string[] }` keyed by Zod schema keys (review-form keys: `themes`/`season`/`location` + closed-enum violations).
  - **(3) Script wrapping scope — SKIP all (user direction "if you think it's best to skip, skip").** Three candidate scripts (`identify-and-restore-missing-lessons.ts`, `import-data.js`, `migrate-metadata-to-columns.mjs`) all read from `consolidated_lessons.json` archive — pre-canonical metadata shapes. Wrapping with `lessonMetadataSchema.parse()` would surface false-positive failures on legitimate legacy shapes the scripts are designed to PRESERVE. Additionally `identify-and-restore-missing-lessons.ts:46-49` has a known activity_type bug (writes `'indoor'`/`'outdoor'` from locationRequirements as if those were activity values; canonical enum is `cooking/garden/both/academic/craft`) that wrapping would expose. All candidates have `requireNonProd` guards so they can never write PROD anyway. Forward-living write coverage achieved at edge function + frontend layers — those ARE the production write paths. Captured as a session decision.
  - **(4) `lessons_with_metadata` view tags projection — already projects `tags`.** Verified at `supabase/migrations/20260512000000_drop_lesson_format.sql` (the view definition committed in Task 1.3, line 36 of the view body: `l.tags,` is a top-level projection). Smart-search and search-lessons edge functions filter via `q.overlaps('tags', filters.tags)` against this column — Session 10's `_shared/search-helpers.ts` change works as-is. NO view change needed.
- **Implementation in 4 file edits / 2 new files (commit `7b27d03`, +322 lines):**
  - **NEW `supabase/functions/_shared/metadataSchemas.ts` (~125 lines).** Deno-runtime mirror of canonical schemas. `import { z } from 'zod'` resolves via `deno.json` (`npm:zod@3.24.0`) on edge AND from `node_modules` in node — dual-runtime by design. Header comment notes the duplication rationale (edge functions can't reliably import from `src/` at deploy time; `_shared/` is the established pattern per `cors.ts`/`search-helpers.ts`). Contains: 4 closed-enum value list constants (ACTIVITY_TYPE_VALUES / TAG_VALUES / SEASON_TIMING_VALUES / CULTURAL_RESPONSIVENESS_FEATURE_VALUES), 4 closed-enum Zod types, 1 academicIntegration union schema (array OR object form), `lessonMetadataSchema` (canonical-keys, ~22 fields), `reviewFormPayloadSchema` (review-form keys: themes/season/location, ~17 fields).
  - **NEW `src/types/edgeSharedSchemas.equivalence.test.ts` (~120 lines, 30 tests).** 4 closed-enum-list equivalence tests (assert `[...sharedX]` equals `[...canonicalX]` for the 4 enums). 9 valid + 6 invalid lesson-metadata fixtures asserting BOTH schemas safeParse identically (success match + data equality on success). 7 valid + 4 invalid review-form-payload fixtures with the same assertion pattern. CI fails if mirror drifts from canonical. Pattern parallels `enums.json.test.ts`.
  - **EDIT `supabase/functions/complete-review/index.ts`** (+22 lines). New import `reviewFormPayloadSchema from '../_shared/metadataSchemas.ts'`. New 17-line block positioned AFTER the existing structural checks (submissionId/decision/selectedLessonId/decision-update-requires-target) and BEFORE the embedding-regen and serviceClient creation. Skips parse when `metadata` is null/undefined/non-object/array (RPC accepts `{}` for non-approve decisions). On `safeParse` failure: returns 400 with `{ error: 'Invalid metadata shape', fieldErrors: flat.fieldErrors, formErrors: flat.formErrors }` (rich shape per user direction).
  - **EDIT `src/pages/ReviewDetail.tsx`** (+46 lines). New import `reviewFormPayloadSchema from '@/types/reviewFormPayload.zod'`. New module-level `ZOD_FIELD_TO_LABEL: Record<string, string>` map (17 keys → human labels: activityType→"Activity Type", season→"Season & Timing", themes→"Thematic Categories", etc., mirroring existing required-fields labels for inline-error consistency). New 23-line block in `handleSaveReview` positioned BETWEEN the existing required-fields-pass clearing (`setValidationErrors([])`/`setSaveError(null)`) and `setSaving(true)`. On Zod failure: `setValidationErrors(invalidLabels)` (so per-IntFormField `fieldError()` highlights the right rows reusing the existing UX) AND `setSaveError(\`Some fields have invalid values:\\n${detailLines.join('\\n')}\`)` (so the reviewer sees specific Zod messages per field) AND `logger.error(...)` AND scroll-to-top. `setSaving(true)` moved to immediately after the new block.
- **One prettier line-wrap auto-fix during lint** — the multi-line arrow function `Object.keys(fieldErrors).map((key) => ZOD_FIELD_TO_LABEL[key] ?? key)` was wrapped across lines by my Edit; prettier collapsed it to one line. No semantic change.
- **Verification (per `superpowers:verification-before-completion`):**
  - `npm run type-check` → green.
  - `npm run lint` → green after one prettier fix-up.
  - `npm test --run` → **537/537 across 38 files** (Session 10 baseline 507/507/37 + 30 new equivalence tests in 1 new file, 0 regressions).
  - `npm run test:rls` → 5 passed / 2 failed (same pre-existing `archive_duplicate_lesson` scenario failures as Sessions 6-10 baseline; Task 1.5 touches no RLS or RPC).
  - **Edge function smoke** via `supabase functions serve complete-review --no-verify-jwt` (background, ~12s warm-up): edge runtime image pulled (v1.73.13, Deno 2.1.4); function loaded; curl probe with fake JWT correctly returned 401 from auth-check (positioned BEFORE Zod validation by design — auth-first request path). Module-load smoke is the load-bearing proof here that `npm:zod@3.24.0` resolves; full-flow Zod smoke (real reviewer JWT, malformed metadata, expect 400 with fieldErrors) defers to PR-open deploy preview.
  - `git diff --stat` confirmed 4 files changed: 2 new (`_shared/metadataSchemas.ts` + `edgeSharedSchemas.equivalence.test.ts`), 2 edited (`complete-review/index.ts` + `ReviewDetail.tsx`). Tooling state files (.beads/, .claude/scheduled_tasks.lock) NOT staged.
- **Decisions captured during execution:**
  - **Inline-error UX over schema-error-only banner.** ReviewDetail's existing required-fields banner says "Missing required fields: A, B"; the IntFormField `fieldError()` per-row helper triggers per-field error styling. Approach kept the existing banner text (since 99% of triggers will be required-fields path) and reused validationErrors for Zod-mapped labels — schema errors get the same per-row red state. Specific Zod messages additionally surface in the saveError banner so the reviewer can SEE exactly what's wrong with each field. Combining banner+inline+saveError covers the full error surface without UX restructure.
  - **`tags` deliberately NOT in ZOD_FIELD_TO_LABEL.** `reviewFormPayloadSchema` doesn't include tags (review form doesn't expose a tags picker today; tags arrive via canonical-keys path / PR 2 LLM draft only). If the reviewer surface ever exposes tags, add to the schema AND the label map together. Mirrors the same decision in Task 1.0's review-form schema.
  - **No script wrapping** (see decision point #3 above) — captured here as the durable principle: forward-living script writes that are ALREADY canonical-shape-clean would benefit from wrapping; legacy-archive-data scripts whose ENTIRE PURPOSE is to preserve historical shapes shouldn't be wrapped because validation against current canonical shape would block legitimate restoration. Future refactor of those scripts (if any) would be the right time to wrap them.
  - **Smoke-test approach.** Module-load proof (function boots without import error) is sufficient evidence that the deno.json `npm:zod@3.24.0` resolution works. Full-flow Zod smoke (real JWT, malformed payload, 400 with fieldErrors) requires either a logged-in reviewer session or a CI deploy. Captured as PR-open verification.
- **`bd doctor` warnings emitted by broken beads tooling during commit** — ignorable per `project_beads_broken.md`.
- **No push.** Per multi-task PR pattern — PR 1 opens after Task 1.6 (CHECK constraints) lands.

Next session: PR 1 Task 1.6 — SQL CHECK + trigger value-validation. Per impl plan §1.6 + Gate A amendment 9. Single migration file with multi-stage operations:
1. **Pre-CHECK CRF drift cleanup** — TEST DB has 1 row (`'Communication of high expectations'`, singular typo of `'Communicates'`); CHECK as spec'd would fail to install. Fold idempotent UPDATE into the SAME migration BEFORE the CHECK installs: `UPDATE lessons SET cultural_responsiveness_features = array_replace(cultural_responsiveness_features, 'Communication of high expectations', 'Communicates high expectations') WHERE 'Communication of high expectations' = ANY(cultural_responsiveness_features);` Re-running this is a no-op (the array no longer contains the old value). Verify on PROD via `mcp__supabase-remote__execute_sql` at PR 1 PROD-apply time — likely ≤1 row to clean in PROD too.
2. **Three CHECK constraints** following `valid_seasons` precedent (set-containment idiom): `CHECK (activity_type <@ ARRAY['cooking','garden','both','academic','craft'])` on `lessons.activity_type` (text[]); `CHECK (tags <@ ARRAY['orientation','bilingual_handouts'])` on `lessons.tags` (text[]); `CHECK (cultural_responsiveness_features <@ ARRAY[...7 master-list features...])` on `lessons.cultural_responsiveness_features` (text[]). Each `IF NOT EXISTS` via DO block for idempotency. Hand-synced from `enums.json` (validator-architecture decision 6); add `-- SOURCE: enums.json["<key>"]` comment markers per validator-arch doc.
3. **Trigger extension** — extend `lessons_normalize_write_trg` (current shape-only coverage of 10 fields) to value-validate JSONB-embedded enum keys (where enums live in `metadata` rather than column). Pattern: `RAISE EXCEPTION` on bad value (hard-fail, not coercion-with-NOTICE which is the current pattern for shape-only). Hand-synced from enums.json. Scope: same 4 closed-enum keys — activity_type / tags / season_timing / cultural_responsiveness_features as they appear in `metadata`.
4. **Forward-rollback `.sql.rollback` sibling file** — drop the constraints + restore prior trigger body. CRF row UPDATE not strictly reversible (the typo'd value is gone); accept.

Verify locally via `supabase db reset` + MCP queries:
- All 3 CHECKs present in `pg_constraint` with the right CHECK clauses;
- INSERT with valid value succeeds; INSERT with invalid value (e.g., `activity_type = ['indoor']`) raises CONSTRAINT violation;
- Trigger raises EXCEPTION on `metadata->>'activityType'` set to `'invalid'` for an UPDATE.

Verify on TEST DB via `mcp__supabase-test__execute_sql` after CI applies (when PR 1 opens).

Decision points to surface at start of Session 12 (Task 1.6 kickoff):
- **Trigger value-validation scope.** Should the trigger validate ALL `metadata`-embedded closed-enum keys (activityType / tags / seasonTiming / culturalResponsivenessFeatures), or only ones that appear in PROD today? Cleanest is "all closed enums" but it could surface drift on legacy rows. The CRF cleanup is one example; do other closed-enum keys have similar drift in metadata? Worth a quick TEST DB audit before locking the trigger scope.
- **Rollback file extension convention.** Task 1.3 used `.sql.rollback` (inert by extension; supabase CLI ignores). Task 1.6 should use the same. Capture in commit if Task 1.2 / 1.4a / 1.4b varied (Task 1.2 used inline comments, Tasks 1.4a/b same).
- **Whether to also CHECK `season_timing` text[] column.** v3 baseline only enforces `valid_seasons` on a single column today. We have a closed enum (4 values) — CHECK installs cleanly. But the design doc only listed 3 CHECKs (activity_type / tags / CRF). Adding a 4th matches the closed-enum coverage logically but expands scope. Lean: include it (consistent with the principle), call it out in the commit.
- **Trigger error message format.** Today's coercion logs `RAISE NOTICE`. New value-validation should use `RAISE EXCEPTION` with a structured message — e.g., `'Invalid value "%s" for metadata->>%s; expected one of %s'`. Worth standardizing the message shape so downstream UI can parse it if needed.

- **Migration shape (per impl plan §1.6 + Gate B sketch):**
  - Stage 1: Pre-CHECK CRF cleanup. Idempotent column-side `array_replace(...)` UPDATE with `WHERE 'Communication of high expectations' = ANY(cultural_responsiveness_features)` filter (no-op on rows that don't have the value). Idempotent metadata-side `jsonb_set(...)` UPDATE rebuilding `culturalResponsivenessFeatures` array element-by-element via `jsonb_agg(CASE WHEN val=...THEN...ELSE val END)` with `@> '"Communication of high expectations"'::jsonb` filter. Order: column UPDATE first (so subsequent CHECK install passes); metadata UPDATE second (covered by pre-existing baseline coverage; no CHECK on the JSON-blob side).
  - Stage 2: Three CHECK constraints via DO-block `pg_constraint` existence checks. `valid_activity_type` (`<@ ARRAY['cooking','garden','both','academic','craft']`), `valid_tags` (`<@ ARRAY['orientation','bilingual_handouts']`), `valid_cultural_responsiveness_features` (`<@` 7-feature master list). Each preceded by a `-- SOURCE: enums.json["<key>"]` marker per validator-arch decision 6 (Gate B output).
  - Stage 3: New helper function `_validate_meta_enum_values(p_meta jsonb, p_key text, p_allowed text[], p_lesson_id text) RETURNS void`. Reads `p_meta->p_key`; no-op on null/jsonb-null. Branches on `jsonb_typeof` — `'string'` case: `(value #>> '{}')` extracted text checked against `ANY(p_allowed)` ; `'array'` case: `SELECT v.value INTO v_invalid_value FROM jsonb_array_elements_text(...) WHERE NOT (...) LIMIT 1`. RAISE EXCEPTION format matches Decision 3 + USING HINT carries `lesson_id=%s`.
  - Stage 4: `lessons_normalize_write` CREATE OR REPLACE. Body byte-identical to `20260512000000_drop_lesson_format.sql` lines 721-968 EXCEPT for the new (V) section between (A) rescue and (C) academic_integration sync. (V) calls `_validate_meta_enum_values` for the 3 keys. Section labels (C)..(K) preserved from `20260509000000` baseline. COMMENT updated to mention the (V) section.
  - Stage 5: Final `NOTIFY pgrst, 'reload schema'` (defensive — no schema-shape changes from PostgREST's perspective; pg_constraint/pg_proc reload precaution).
- **Coordinated `seed.sql` edit (folded into the Task 1.6 commit per Session 7 precedent).** Initial `supabase db reset` failed with `valid_activity_type` CHECK violation on seed insert because the 5 sample lessons used Title Case `'Cooking'` / `'Gardening'` (not in canonical enum). Note `Gardening` → `garden` (canonical drops the -ing). Status doc Session 9 had pre-flagged this divergence ("local seed lessons have Title-Case `Cooking`/`Gardening` values rather than PROD-corpus lowercase"). Captured as a Task 1.6 commit-folding decision because `db reset` is the verification path for ALL Task 1.6 smokes — it's a verification dependency, not a clean separation.

Process learnings (Session 13):
- **Multi-reviewer split by surface beats single-reviewer with cross-cutting focus.** 8-commit diff across SQL / Zod / frontend was too broad for one agent to go deep on each surface; coverage went shallow when pilot-tested in advance. 3 parallel agents with surface-scoped briefs returned ~30 file-level reads each + comprehensive focus-area sign-off. Total runtime ~5-6 minutes parallel (vs ~10-15 minutes serial estimated). Pattern reusable for future multi-task PRs.
- **Reviewer line-number citations need verification before action.** Reviewer C cited specific line numbers for hand-patch fixes that turned out to refer to a sibling table (`lesson_archive`) rather than the named target (`lessons`). The grep output did show 9 `lesson_format` occurrences across 3 distinct table blocks, and Reviewer C's table identification reversed which lines were which. Spot-check via Read before applying line-targeted edits is mandatory, not optional.
- **`supabase gen types` produces high-noise diffs across CLI version drift.** When the existing types file was generated by an older CLI, full regen produces formatting churn (~3000 lines) that buries the actual schema changes. The repo's hand-patch precedent (chore(types): patch database.types.ts ...) is the right pattern for incremental schema changes. Full regen should be deferred to a dedicated cleanup PR (when the cosmetic changes are the point, not the side effect).
- **Re-running `supabase db reset` after editing an unpushed migration is a fast verification path.** Verified the `NOTIFY pgrst` addition to migration 1.2 applied cleanly across all 59 migrations on a fresh local DB. CI on TEST DB will pick up the same change when migrations apply on PR open (the modified migration row in `supabase_migrations.schema_migrations` only matters once it's been applied; pre-push edits to unpushed migrations are safe per `supabase/migrations/CLAUDE.md`).

Next session: Session 14 — PR 1 ritual round 2. See "In flight" section above for the full step-by-step. Key decision points likely to surface: (a) which findings to accept vs reject across the 4 PR comment surfaces; (b) whether any finding requires DB-affecting fix-ups (which mandates per-round TEST DB re-verification); (c) round-cap decision after 2 review rounds. The `feedback_workflows_not_sacred.md` mode of "open to redesign at workflow level" is unlikely to apply here — PR 1 is mostly a schema migration PR, and any workflow redesign would have been raised during the pre-PR walkthrough (it wasn't).

Three reasons: portability between TEST/PROD (hardcoded list breaks if DBs diverge in future; pattern-based works regardless — TEST/PROD audit returned identical IDs but that's a snapshot, not a guarantee), idempotency + forward safety (re-run is no-op), stays out of Stage 1 worksheet territory (case canonicalization for seasonTiming deferred per Session 12 Decision 2). SR-B's WHERE clause is the load-bearing piece that makes this migration portable.
